## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p88/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S
SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
NUM_GROUPS = 256
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
EPS = 1e-05

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
                acc += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert(acc + S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32), S.bf16)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += d * d
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, multiply_weight_shape):
        super().__init__()
        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
        self.multiply_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(multiply_weight_shape))

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or self.group_norm.num_groups != NUM_GROUPS or (self.group_norm.eps != EPS) or (tuple(self.multiply_weight.shape) != (OUT_FEATURES,)):
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        w_t = self.gemm.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        bias = self.gemm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        mul = self.multiply_weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x.contiguous(), w_t, bias, gn_w, gn_b, mul, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S
SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
NUM_GROUPS = 256
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
EPS = 1e-05

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
                acc += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert(acc + S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32), S.bf16)
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += d * d
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t

                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, multiply_weight_shape):
        super().__init__()

        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)

        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_cuda_nvidia


@substrate.jit
def gemm_2stages_pipeline(
    A: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
    B: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
    C: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
):
    MMA_M = 16
    MMA_N = 8
    MMA_K = 16

    WARP_SIZE = 32

    # Work group configuration
    WARPS_M = 2  # Number of warps in M dimension per work group
    WARPS_N = 2  # Number of warps in N dimension per work group

    # Each warp computes multiple MMA tiles
    MMA_TILES_M = 2  # Number of MMA tiles per warp in M dimension
    MMA_TILES_N = 2  # Number of MMA tiles per warp in N dimension

    # Block size
    BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M  # Total M covered by work group
    BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N  # Total N covered by work group

    K_tiles = 8  # 128 // 16

    # =========================================== #

    # Work group and warp identification
    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)
    warp_id = thread_id >> 5  # thread_id // WARP_SIZE
    lane_id = thread_id % WARP_SIZE

    warp_row_id = warp_id >> 1  # warp_id // WARPS_N
    warp_col_id = warp_id % WARPS_N

    # Shared memory: [stage][warp_row][warp_col][local_row][local_col]
    # A: [2][WARPS_M][MMA_TILES_M][MMA_M][MMA_K]
    # B: [2][WARPS_N][MMA_TILES_N][MMA_N][MMA_K]
    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 16, 16), S.f16)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 8, 16), S.f16)
    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 2, 16, 8), S.f16)

    # Accumulators for each MMA tile this warp computes
    RC = S.make_local((2, 2, 4), S.f16)

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for i in S.range(4):
                RC[tm, tn, i] = S.convert(0, S.f16)

    # Precompute addressing for A and B loads
    row_a = lane_id >> 1
    col_a = (lane_id & 1) * 8
    row_b = (lane_id % (MMA_N * 2)) >> 1
    col_b = ((lane_id % (MMA_N * 2)) & 1) * 8

    # Stage 0: Prefetch first tile (k_tile = 0) into buffer 0
    write_stage = 0
    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for j in S.range(8):
            global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + row_a
            global_col = col_a + j
            a_smem[write_stage, warp_row_id, tm, row_a, col_a + j] = A[global_row, global_col]

    for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
        for j in S.range(8):
            global_row = col_b + j
            global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + row_b
            b_smem[write_stage, warp_col_id, tn, row_b, col_b + j] = B[global_row, global_col]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Main pipeline loop
    for k_tile in S.range(K_tiles - 1):
        read_stage = k_tile & 1
        write_stage = 1 - read_stage

        # Prefetch next tile
        next_k = k_tile + 1
        for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
            for j in S.range(8):
                global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + row_a
                global_col = next_k * MMA_K + col_a + j
                a_smem[write_stage, warp_row_id, tm, row_a, col_a + j] = A[global_row, global_col]

        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for j in S.range(8):
                global_row = next_k * MMA_K + col_b + j
                global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + row_b
                b_smem[write_stage, warp_col_id, tn, row_b, col_b + j] = B[global_row, global_col]

        # Compute all MMA tiles for this warp
        for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
            for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
                # Load A tile
                a_row_offset = lane_id % 16
                a_col_offset = (lane_id >> 4) * 8
                a_smem_tile = S.subview(a_smem, (read_stage, warp_row_id, tm, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 16, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
                a_tile_2d = S.subview(a_smem_tile, (a_row_offset, a_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
                RA = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x4_b16(a_tile_2d)

                # Load B tile
                b_row_offset = lane_id % 8
                b_col_offset = ((lane_id >> 3) & 1) * 8
                b_smem_tile = S.subview(b_smem, (read_stage, warp_col_id, tn, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 8, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
                b_tile_2d = S.subview(b_smem_tile, (b_row_offset, b_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
                RB = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x2_b16(b_tile_2d)

                # MMA
                RC_view = S.subview(RC, (tm, tn, 0), (1, 1, 4), (1, 1, 1))
                RC_result = S.nvvm.mma_16x8x16_f16_f16(RA, RB, RC_view)

                # Store back to RC
                for i in S.range(4):
                    RC[tm, tn, i] = RC_result[i]

        S.syncthreads()

    # Handle the last k_tile
    last_stage = (K_tiles - 1) & 1

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            # Load A tile
            a_row_offset = lane_id % 16
            a_col_offset = (lane_id >> 4) * 8
            a_smem_tile_last = S.subview(
                a_smem, (last_stage, warp_row_id, tm, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 16, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1)
            )
            a_tile_2d_last = S.subview(a_smem_tile_last, (a_row_offset, a_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
            RA = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x4_b16(a_tile_2d_last)

            # Load B tile
            b_row_offset = lane_id % 8
            b_col_offset = ((lane_id >> 3) & 1) * 8
            b_smem_tile_last = S.subview(b_smem, (last_stage, warp_col_id, tn, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 8, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
            b_tile_2d_last = S.subview(b_smem_tile_last, (b_row_offset, b_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
            RB = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x2_b16(b_tile_2d_last)

            # MMA
            RC_view = S.subview(RC, (tm, tn, 0), (1, 1, 4), (1, 1, 1))
            RC_result = S.nvvm.mma_16x8x16_f16_f16(RA, RB, RC_view)

            # Store back to RC
            for i in S.range(4):
                RC[tm, tn, i] = RC_result[i]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Store results to shared memory
    row1 = lane_id >> 2
    col1 = (lane_id & 3) * 2

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1, col1] = RC[tm, tn, 0]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1, col1 + 1] = RC[tm, tn, 1]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1 + 8, col1] = RC[tm, tn, 2]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1 + 8, col1 + 1] = RC[tm, tn, 3]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Write results to global memory
    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for j in S.range(MMA_N):
                global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + (lane_id % MMA_M)
                global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + j
                C[global_row, global_col] = c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, (lane_id % MMA_M), j]

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
+        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_u32 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_u32 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_u32[i] = a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane, i]
+            b_frag_u32[i] = b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane, i]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M

+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
+        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_u32 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_u32 = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_u32[i] = a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane, i]
+            b_frag_u32[i] = b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane, i]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
+        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2

+        for i in S.range(4):

+
+        S.syncthreads()

+

+    S.syncthreads()

+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2

+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):

-                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):

+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
+        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
+        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

    36	    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
    37	
    38	
    39	@substrate.jit
    40	def gemm_mfma_kernel(
    41	    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    42	    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    43	    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    44	    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    45	):
    46	    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    47	    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    48	
    49	    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    50	    warp_id = tid >> 5
    51	    lane = tid & 63
    52	    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
    53	    warp_col = warp_id & 1
    54	
    55	    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
    56	    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
    57	    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    58	
    59	    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
    60	    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
    61	    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
    62	    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    63	
    64	    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
    65	        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
    66	        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
    67	        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
    68	        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
    69	        for i in S.range(4):
    70	            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
    71	
    72	        b_chunk_col = tid >> 1
    73	        b_chunk_row = (tid & 1) * 8
    74	        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
    75	        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
    76	        for i in S.range(4):
    77	            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
    78	
    79	        S.syncthreads()
    80	
    81	        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    82	        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    83	
    84	        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
    85	        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
    86	
    87	        S.syncthreads()
    88	
    89	    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
    90	    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
    91	    for mi in S.range(4):
    92	        for ni in S.range(4):
    93	            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
    94	
    95	    S.syncthreads()
    96	
    97	    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
    98	    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
    99	    for j in S.range(2):
   100	        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
   101	        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
   102	        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
   103	        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
   104	
   105	
   106	@substrate.jit
   107	def epilogue_kernel(
   108	    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
   109	    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
   110	    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
   111	    MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
   112	    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
   113	):
   114	    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
   115	    row = S.block_id(0)
   116	    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
   117	        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
   118	        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
   119	            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
   120	            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
   121	        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
   122	
   123	        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
   124	        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
   125	            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
   126	            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
   127	            var += d * d
   128	        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
   129	        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
   130	
   131	        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
   132	            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
   133	            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
   134	            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
   135	            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
   136	            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
   137	            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
   138	            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
   139	
   140	
   141	class ModelNew(nn.Module):
   142	    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, multiply_weight_shape):
   143	        super().__init__()
   144	        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
   145	        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
   146	        self.multiply_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(multiply_weight_shape))
   147	
   148	    def forward(self, x):
   149	        if (
   150	            tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES)
   151	            or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16
   152	            or self.group_norm.num_groups != NUM_GROUPS
   153	            or self.group_norm.eps != EPS
   154	            or tuple(self.multiply_weight.shape) != (OUT_FEATURES,)
   155	        ):
   156	            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
   157	
   158	        x_in = x.contiguous()
   159	        w_t = self.gemm.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
   160	        bias = self.gemm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
   161	        gn_w = self.group_norm.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
   162	        gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
   163	        mul = self.multiply_weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
   164	
   165	        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
   166	        out = torch.empty_like(y)
   167	
   168	        gemm_mfma_kernel[_gemm_launch](x_in, w_t, bias, y)
   169	        epilogue_kernel[_epilogue_launch](y, gn_w, gn_b, mul, out)
   170	        return out

+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_group = tid >> 6
+        b_lane64 = tid & 63
+        b_chunk_row = b_lane64 >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = b_group * 32 + (b_lane64 & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):

+

+

+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()

+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):

+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2

+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_group = tid >> 6
+        b_lane64 = tid & 63
+        b_chunk_row = b_lane64 >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = b_group * 32 + (b_lane64 & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
+
 SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192

@@ -13,40 +12,135 @@
 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_group = tid >> 6
+        b_lane64 = tid & 63
+        b_chunk_row = b_lane64 >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = b_group * 32 + (b_lane64 & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS

+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_group = tid >> 6
+        b_lane64 = tid & 63
+        b_chunk_row = b_lane64 >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = b_group * 32 + (b_lane64 & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

+WARP_SIZE = 32
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((128, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[tid, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_group = tid >> 6
+        b_lane64 = tid & 63
+        b_chunk_row = b_lane64 >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = b_group * 32 + (b_lane64 & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[tid, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_row * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_col * 64 + lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

codex
The sparse probe shows the current MFMA operand packing is structurally wrong, not just slightly permuted. I’m fixing that at the LDS-fragment level: stage row-major tiles in shared memory, then assemble the interleaved `4+4` BF16 halves from LDS before the two MFMA steps.

-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((64, 16), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((16, 64), S.bf16)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        a_vals = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + i] = a_vals[0, i, 0]
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + 4 + i] = a_vals[1, i, 0]
+
+        b_chunk_row = tid >> 3
+        b_chunk_col = (tid & 7) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[b_chunk_row, b_chunk_col + i] = b_vals[0, i, 0]
+            b_smem[b_chunk_row, b_chunk_col + 4 + i] = b_vals[1, i, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_col_group = (lane & 1) * 4
+        b_col = lane >> 1
+        b_row_group = (lane & 1) * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag[0, i, 0] = a_smem[warp_row * 32 + a_row, a_col_group + i]
+            a_frag[1, i, 0] = a_smem[warp_row * 32 + a_row, 8 + a_col_group + i]
+            b_frag[0, i, 0] = b_smem[b_row_group + i, warp_col * 32 + b_col]
+            b_frag[1, i, 0] = b_smem[8 + b_row_group + i, warp_col * 32 + b_col]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(

+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))

+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1

+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2

+        a_vals = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + i] = a_vals[0, i, 0]
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + 4 + i] = a_vals[1, i, 0]
+

+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)

+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 5
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((64, 16), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((16, 64), S.bf16)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = tid >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (tid & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        a_vals = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + i] = a_vals[0, i, 0]
+            a_smem[a_chunk_row, a_chunk_col + 4 + i] = a_vals[1, i, 0]
+
+        b_chunk_row = tid >> 3
+        b_chunk_col = (tid & 7) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[b_chunk_row, b_chunk_col + i] = b_vals[0, i, 0]
+            b_smem[b_chunk_row, b_chunk_col + 4 + i] = b_vals[1, i, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_col_group = (lane & 1) * 4
+        b_col = lane >> 1
+        b_row_group = (lane & 1) * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag[0, i, 0] = a_smem[warp_row * 32 + a_row, a_col_group + i]
+            a_frag[1, i, 0] = a_smem[warp_row * 32 + a_row, 8 + a_col_group + i]
+            b_frag[0, i, 0] = b_smem[b_row_group + i, warp_col * 32 + b_col]
+            b_frag[1, i, 0] = b_smem[8 + b_row_group + i, warp_col * 32 + b_col]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def epilogue_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
     one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
-                acc += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(acc + S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32), S.bf16)
-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
-            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
-            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
-                var += d * d
-            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

codex
I found a more fundamental issue: the wave count was wrong. `mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` is a 64-lane wave op, so a 2x2 wave grid needs `256` threads, not `128`. I’m correcting the block shape and simplifying the operand staging back to per-wave invariant chunks.
apply patch

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S

 IN_FEATURES = 8192

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 32, 32), S.f32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_base + mi, col_base + ni] = acc[mi * 4 + ni]
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_in_warp = tid >> 1
+    col_pair = (tid & 1) * 2
+    for j in S.range(2):
+        out_row = block_m + row_in_warp
+        out_col = block_n + col_pair + j
+        value = c_smem[warp_row, warp_col, row_in_warp - warp_row * 32, col_pair + j + warp_col * 32]
+        Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

+def epilogue_kernel(

+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

Memory access fault by GPU node-7 (Agent handle: 0x3b357100) on address 0x7eba92c07000. Reason: Write access to a read-only page.

codex
The GPU fault is in the current writeback path, which was still sized for `128` threads. I’m switching to direct per-lane global stores from the MFMA accumulators using the same 4x4 tile assumption, which removes the broken block-wide writeback logic.
apply patch

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
+

 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192

@@ -13,40 +12,124 @@
 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+

 @substrate.jit
-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def epilogue_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
     one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
-    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):

-        for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):

-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                mean += S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32)
-            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                d = S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean
-                var += d * d
-            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
