-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
 
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))

+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))

+
+        x_in = x.contiguous()

         bias = self.gemm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
         gn_w = self.group_norm.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
         gn_b = self.group_norm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
         mul = self.multiply_weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+

+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):

+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):

+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

+        S.syncthreads()

+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

        print('"'row',i,[(j,float(vals[i,j])) for j in nz])

-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, lane, i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_u32 = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_frag_u32 = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 2
+        b_group = lane & 3
+        a_frag_u32[0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_u32[1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_u32[2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_u32[3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_u32[2] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 8 + b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[3] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 9 + b_group * 2]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

+    row = S.block_id(0)

+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2

+WAVE_TILE_N = 32

+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K

+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_u32 = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_frag_u32 = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 2
+        b_group = lane & 3
+        a_frag_u32[0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_u32[1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_u32[2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_u32[3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_u32[2] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 8 + b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_u32[3] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 9 + b_group * 2]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_u32, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

codex
The remaining blocker is substrate’s lowering for `mfma(view(make_local(...)))`. I’m moving the assembled `4-u32` fragments back through shared memory so the final MFMA operands are loaded from LDS exactly as shared slices, which the local example path does lower.
apply patch

+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N

+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K

+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 2
+        b_group = lane & 3
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 8 + b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 9 + b_group * 2]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 2
+        b_group = lane & 3
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 8 + b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 9 + b_group * 2]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+

+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 8 + b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, 9 + b_group * 2]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+

codex
The current B assembly is still collapsing the N coverage too aggressively. I’m changing just the B-fragment gather to an `8 row-groups x 8 col-groups` interpretation, where each 16-byte LDS fragment interleaves the same 4-column group from K rows `0..7` and `8..15`.
apply patch

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 3
+        b_group = lane & 7
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]

+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 3
+        b_group = lane & 7
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(

+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+

+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):

+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8

+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):

+

+

+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 3

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S

 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * WAVE_TILE_M
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * WAVE_TILE_N
+BLOCK_K = 16
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 3
+        b_group = lane & 7
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)
+
+
 @substrate.jit
-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
+def epilogue_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    MUL_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

-            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)

-                var += d * d
-            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

-                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
-                v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
-                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    for g in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32)
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+        inv_std = one / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+        for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
+            v = (S.convert(Y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) * inv_std
+            v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            v = v * S.convert(MUL_WEIGHT[c], S.f32)
+            v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+            OUT[row, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+WARP_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+WAVE_TILE_M = 32
+WAVE_TILE_N = 32

+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K

+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+
+def _epilogue_launch():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((4, 32, 8), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((4, 16, 16), S.u32)
+    a_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_frag_smem = S.make_shared((4, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_chunk_row = lane >> 1
+        a_chunk_col = (lane & 1) * 8
+        a_offset = ((block_m + warp_row * 32 + a_chunk_row) * IN_FEATURES + k_tile * BLOCK_K + a_chunk_col) * 2
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_smem[warp_id, a_chunk_row, (lane & 1) * 4 + i] = a_packed[i]
+
+        b_chunk_row = lane >> 2
+        b_chunk_col = (lane & 3) * 8
+        b_offset = ((k_tile * BLOCK_K + b_chunk_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_n + warp_col * 32 + b_chunk_col) * 2
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            b_smem[warp_id, b_chunk_row, (lane & 3) * 4 + i] = b_packed[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row = lane >> 1
+        a_group = lane & 1
+        b_row = lane >> 3
+        b_group = lane & 7
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, a_group * 2 + 1]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 4 + a_group * 2]
+        a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = a_smem[warp_id, a_row, 5 + a_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 0] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 1] = b_smem[warp_id, b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 2] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2]
+        b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane, 3] = b_smem[warp_id, 8 + b_row, b_group * 2 + 1]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_frag_smem[warp_id, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    row_base = (lane >> 3) * 4
+    col_base = (lane & 7) * 4
+    for mi in S.range(4):
+        out_row = block_m + warp_row * 32 + row_base + mi
+        for ni in S.range(4):
+            out_col = block_n + warp_col * 32 + col_base + ni
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[mi * 4 + ni] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32), S.bf16)

I also ran the required evaluation command. The kernel compiles and runs, but it does not pass correctness yet: the current failure is an MFMA operand/output layout mismatch, not a compile/runtime failure. The latest round-local result is in [debug_eval.jsonl](/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p88/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/debug_eval.jsonl).
